The exact concatenation order and final context can be inspected from the ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"/memory"}]," dialog. The typical loading order is:\n",["$","ol",null,{"className":"x:[:is(ol,ul)_&]:my-[.75em] x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:list-decimal x:ms-6","children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Global Context File:"}],"\n",["$","ul",null,{"className":"x:[:is(ol,ul)_&]:my-[.75em] x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:list-disc x:ms-[1.5em]","children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":["Location: ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"~/.qwen/<configured-context-filename>"}]," (e.g., ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"~/.qwen/QWEN.md"}]," in your user home directory)."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":"Scope: Provides default instructions for all your projects."}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Project Root & Ancestors Context Files:"}],"\n",["$","ul",null,{"className":"x:[:is(ol,ul)_&]:my-[.75em] x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:list-disc x:ms-[1.5em]","children":["\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":["Location: The CLI searches for the configured context file in the current working directory and then in each parent directory up to either the project root (identified by a ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":".git"}]," folder) or your home directory."]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":"Scope: Provides context relevant to the entire project or a significant portion of it."}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n"]}],"\n",["$","li",null,{"className":"x:my-[.5em]","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Concatenation & UI Indication:"}]," The contents of all found context files are concatenated (with separators indicating their origin and path) and provided as part of the system prompt.
